<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Flag_of_Australia_%28converted%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Australia_%28converted%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Flag_of_Australia_%28converted%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Australia_%28converted%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Flag_of_Australia_%28converted%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_Australia_%28converted%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1280" data-file-height="640" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>
</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/Fox_League" title="Fox League">Fox League</a>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Radio">Radio</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Super_League&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Radio">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Talksport" title="Talksport">Talksport</a> is an official broadcaster of Super League, broadcasting commentaries and magazine programming on Talksport 2. <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_5_Live_Sports_Extra" title="BBC Radio 5 Live Sports Extra">BBC Radio 5 Live Sports Extra</a> covers more than 70 Super League games through <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_5_Live" title="BBC Radio 5 Live">5 Live</a> Rugby League each Thursday and Friday night.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Each 3 hour programme is presented by <a href="/wiki/Dave_Woods_(commentator)" title="Dave Woods (commentator)">Dave Woods</a> with a guest summariser (usually a Super League player or coach) and in addition to live commentary also includes interviews and debate. A <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_5_Live" title="BBC Radio 5 Live">5 Live</a> Rugby League podcast is available to download each week from the BBC website at <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/programmes/p02nrtxd/episodes/downloads">http://www.bbc.co.uk/programmes/p02nrtxd/episodes/downloads</a>.
</p><p>Super League is also covered extensively by <a href="/wiki/BBC_Local_Radio" title="BBC Local Radio">BBC Local Radio</a>:
</p>
<table class="wikitable">

<tbody><tr>
<th>Station
</th>
<th>Area
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_Humberside" title="BBC Radio Humberside">BBC Radio Humberside</a>
</td>
<td>Hull
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_Leeds" title="BBC Radio Leeds">BBC Radio Leeds</a>
</td>
<td>West Yorkshire
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_Manchester" title="BBC Radio Manchester">BBC Radio Manchester</a>
</td>
<td>Salford, Wigan and Warrington.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_Merseyside" title="BBC Radio Merseyside">BBC Radio Merseyside</a>
</td>
<td>St Helens, Warrington and Widnes.
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The competition is also covered on commercial radio stations:
</p>
<ul><li>Radio Yorkshire cover two matches per round featuring Yorkshire clubs.</li>
<li>BCB 106.6 (Bradford Community Broadcasting) have full match commentary on Bradford home and away.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wish_FM" title="Wish FM">Wish FM</a> have full match commentary on Wigan and St Helens matches home and away.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Wire_FM" title="Wire FM">Wire FM</a> have full match commentary of Warrington amatches home and away.</li>
<li>Grand Sud FM covers every Catalans Dragons Home Match (in French).</li>
<li>Radio France Bleu Roussillon covers every Catalans Dragons Away Match (in French).</li></ul>
<p>All Super League commentaries on any station are available via the particular stations on-line streaming.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Internet">Internet</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Super_League&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Internet">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/ESPN3" title="ESPN3">ESPN3</a>, formerly ESPN360, has had worldwide broadband rights since 2007 when they broadcast the 2007 Grand Final.
</p><p>Since 9 April 2009, all of the matches shown on Sky Sports have also been available live online via <a href="/wiki/Livestation" class="mw-redirect" title="Livestation">Livestation</a> everywhere in the world excluding the US, Puerto Rico, UK, Ireland, France, Monaco, Australia and New Zealand.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> In 2016 Livestation shut down, however these matches are also available online for UK users only through <a href="/wiki/Sky_Go" title="Sky Go">Sky Go</a> and <a href="/wiki/Now_TV_(UK)" class="mw-redirect" title="Now TV (UK)">Now TV</a>.
</p><p>In the United Kingdom, a number of commercial radio stations, along with <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_5_Live_Sports_Extra" title="BBC Radio 5 Live Sports Extra">BBC Radio 5 Live Sports Extra</a> and the local BBC radio stations simulcast commentary of Super League games on the internet. Additionally, the <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_5_Live" title="BBC Radio 5 Live">5 Live</a> Rugby League podcast is available to download each week from the BBC website at <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/programmes/p02nrtxd/episodes/downloads">http://www.bbc.co.uk/programmes/p02nrtxd/episodes/downloads</a>.
</p>
